PDF Export button triggers window.print()', async ({ page }) => {\n  test.slow();\n  await page.goto(BASE_URL);\n\n  // Export PDF button should be disabled initially\n  const exportBtn = page.getByRole('button', { name: /export pdf/i });\n  await expect(exportBtn).toBeDisabled();\n\n  // Format a document first\n  const textarea = await getTextarea(page);\n  await textarea.fill(RESUME_TEXT);\n  await (await getFormatButton(page)).click();\n  await expect(page.getByText('Alex Rivera', { exact: false })).toBeVisible({ timeout: 90_000 });\n\n  // Export PDF button should now be enabled\n  await expect(exportBtn).toBeEnabled({ timeout: 10_000 });\n\n  // Intercept window.print()\n  let printCalled = false;\n  await page.exposeFunction('__testPrintCalled', () => { printCalled = true; });\n  await page.evaluate(() => {\n    const orig = window.print.bind(window);\n    window.print = () => {\n      (window as any).__testPrintCalled();\n      // Don't actually print in headless\n    };\n  });\n\n  await exportBtn.click();\n  await page.waitForTimeout(1000);\n  expect(printCalled).toBe(true);\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 6. I need to: 1. Update the tests to handle this error state correctly 2. Update the tests to test for this error as well 3.
